My Reservations Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reservations\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `my-reservations-page` - Div - Container for the reservations page.\n  - `reservations-table` - Table - Displays reservations with date, time, party size, status.\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` - Button - Cancel a specific reservation.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 6. Waitlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Waitlist\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `waitlist-page` - Div - Container for the waitlist page.\n  - `waitlist-party-size` - Dropdown - Select party size.\n  - `join-waitlist-button` - Button - Join the waitlist.\n  - `user-position` - Div - Displays user's current position on waitlist.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 7. My Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reviews\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reviews-page` - Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - `reviews-list` - Div - Lists reviews with dish name, rating, and text.\n  - `write-new-review-button` - Button - Navigate to Write Review page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 8. Write Review Page\n- **Page Title**: Write Review\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `write-review-page` - Div - Container for write review page.\n  - `select-dish` - Dropdown - Select dish to review.\n  - `rating-input` - Dropdown - Select rating 1-5 stars.\n  - `review-text` - Textarea - Input for review text.\n  - `submit-review-button` - Button - Submit review.\n  - `back-to-reviews` - Button - Navigate back to My Reviews page.\n\n### 9. User Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: My Profile\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `profile-page` - Div - Container for profile page.\n  - `profile-username` - Div - Display username (non-editable).\n  - `profile-email` - Input - Update email.\n  - `update-profile-button` - Button - Save profile changes.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n---\n\n## Navigation Flow\n\n- From Dashboard:\n  - `make-reservation-button` -> Make Reservation page\n  - `view-menu-button` -> Menu page\n  - `my-reservations-button` -> My Reservations page\n  - `my-reviews-button` -> My Reviews page\n  - `waitlist-button` -> Waitlist page\n  - `profile-button` -> User Profile page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` refreshes Dashboard\n\n- From Menu page:\n  - `view-dish-button-{dish_id}` -> Dish Details page for selected dish\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Dish Details page:\n  - `back-to-menu` -> Menu page\n\n- From Make Reservation page:\n  - `submit-reservation-button` -> Submit reservation and return to Dashboard\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reservations page:\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` -> Cancel reservation (remains on page or refresh)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Waitlist page:\n  - `join-waitlist-button` -> Join waitlist (user stays on page to see position)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reviews page:\n  - `write-new-review-button` -> Write Review page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Write Review page:\n  - `submit-review-button` -> Submit review and return to My Reviews page\n  - `back-to-reviews` -> My Reviews page\n\n- From User Profile page:\n  - `update-profile-button` -> Save changes (stay or return to Dashboard)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n---\n\n## Data File Schemas\n\nAll data files are stored in the `data/` directory with pipe (`|`) delimited fields. Each line represents one record.\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- Fields: `username|email|phone|full_name`\n- Types:\n  - username: string\n  - email: string\n  - phone: string\n  - full_name: string\n- Example:\n  ```\n  john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner\n  jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie\n  ```\n\n### 2. menu.txt\n- Fields: `dish_id|name|category|price|description|ingredients|dietary|avg_rating`\n- Types:\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - name: string\n  - category: string\n  - price: float\n  - description: string\n  - ingredients: string (comma-separated list)\n  - dietary: string\n  - avg_rating: float\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5\n  2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8\n  3|Chocolate Lava Cake|Desserts|7.99|Warm chocolate cake with molten center|Chocolate,Flour,Eggs,Sugar|Vegetarian|4.9\n  4|Green Tea|Beverages|3.99|Premium Japanese green tea|Green Tea Leaves,Water|Vegan|4.6\n  ```\n\n### 3. reservations.txt\n- Fields: `reservation_id|username|guest_name|phone|email|party_size|date|time|special_requests|status`\n- Types:\n  - reservation_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - guest_name: string\n  - phone: string\n  - email: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - time: time (HH:MM)\n  - special_requests: string\n  - status: string (e.g., Upcoming, Completed)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming\n  2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed\n  3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming\n  ```\n\n### 4. waitlist.txt\n- Fields: `waitlist_id|username|party_size|join_time|status`\n- Types:\n  - waitlist_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - join_time: datetime (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS)\n  - status: string (e.g., Active)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active\n  2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active\n  ```\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Fields: `review_id|username|dish_id|rating|review_text|review_date`\n- Types:\n  - review_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - rating: integer (1-5)\n  - review_text: string\n  - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21\n  2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20\n  3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19\n  ```\n\n---\n\nThis completes the design specification for the RestaurantReservation web application, covering page layouts, element IDs, navigation, and local data file schemas.\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for 'RestaurantReservation' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named 'RestaurantReservation' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse restaurant menus, make table reservations, write reviews, check waitlist status, and manage their dining history. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the 'RestaurantReservation' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe 'RestaurantReservation' web application will consist of the following nine pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured dishes, upcoming reservations, and navigation to other functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: welcome-message** - Type: H1 - Welcome message displaying username.\n  - **ID: make-reservation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to reservation page.\n  - **ID: view-menu-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to menu page.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.\n  - **ID: my-reservations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to my reservations page.\n  - **ID: my-reviews-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to my reviews page.\n  - **ID: waitlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to waitlist page.\n  - **ID: profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to user profile page.\n\n### 2. Menu Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu\n- **Overview**: A page displaying the restaurant menu with categories and filtering.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: menu-page** - Type: Div - Container for the menu page.\n  - **ID: menu-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying dish cards with image, name, price, description.\n  - **ID: view-dish-button-{dish_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view dish details (each card has this).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 3. Dish Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Dish Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific dish.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dish-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dish details page.\n  - **ID: dish-name** - Type: H1 - Display dish name.\n  - **ID: dish-price** - Type: Div - Display dish price.\n  - **ID: back-to-menu** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to menu.\n\n### 4. Make Reservation Page\n- **Page Title**: Make Reservation\n- **Overview**: A page for users to make a table reservation.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: reservation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reservation page.\n  - **ID: guest-name** - Type: Input - Field to input guest name.\n  - **ID: party-size** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select party size (1-10).\n  - **ID: reservation-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select reservation date.\n  - **ID: submit-reservation-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit reservation.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 5. My Reservations Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reservations\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all reservations made by the user.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: my-reservations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my reservations page.\n  - **ID: reservations-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying reservations with date, time, party size, status.\n  - **ID: cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel reservation (each upcoming reservation has this).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 6. Waitlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Waitlist\n- **Overview**: A page for users to join the waitlist and check their position.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: waitlist-page** - Type: Div - Container for the waitlist page.\n  - **ID: waitlist-party-size** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select party size.\n  - **ID: join-waitlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to join waitlist.\n  - **ID: user-position** - Type: Div - Display user's current position in waitlist.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 7. My Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reviews\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all reviews written by the user.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of reviews with dish name, rating, review text.\n  - **ID: write-new-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 8. Write Review Page\n- **Page Title**: Write Review\n- **Overview**: A page for users to write a review for a dish.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: write-review-page** - Type: Div - Container for the write review page.\n  - **ID: select-dish** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select dish to review.\n  - **ID: rating-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select rating (1-5 stars).\n  - **ID: review-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to write review text.\n  - **ID: submit-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit review.\n  - **ID: back-to-reviews** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to my reviews.\n\n### 9. User Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: My Profile\n- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.\n  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).\n  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.\n  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe 'RestaurantReservation' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. User Data\n- **File Name**: `users.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  username|email|phone|full_name\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner\n  jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie\n  ```\n\n### 2. Menu Items Data\n- **File Name**: `menu.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  dish_id|name|category|price|description|ingredients|dietary|avg_rating\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5\n  2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8\n  3|Chocolate Lava Cake|Desserts|7.99|Warm chocolate cake with molten center|Chocolate,Flour,Eggs,Sugar|Vegetarian|4.9\n  4|Green Tea|Beverages|3.99|Premium Japanese green tea|Green Tea Leaves,Water|Vegan|4.6\n  ```\n\n### 3. Reservations Data\n- **File Name**: `reservations.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  reservation_id|username|guest_name|phone|email|party_size|date|time|special_requests|status\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming\n  2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed\n  3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming\n  ```\n\n### 4. Waitlist Data\n- **File Name**: `waitlist.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  waitlist_id|username|party_size|join_time|status\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active\n  2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active\n  ```\n\n### 5. Reviews Data\n- **File Name**: `reviews.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  review_id|username|dish_id|rating|review_text|review_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21\n  2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20\n  3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19\n  ```\n\nAll files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing.\n\n\n=== design_spec.md ===\n# RestaurantReservation Web Application Design Specification\n\n---\n\n## Page Layouts and Elements\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Dashboard\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dashboard-page` - Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - `welcome-message` - H1 - Displays welcome message with username.\n  - `make-reservation-button` - Button - Navigates to Make Reservation page.\n  - `view-menu-button` - Button - Navigates to Menu page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Refreshes or navigates to Dashboard page.\n  - `my-reservations-button` - Button - Navigates to My Reservations page.\n  - `my-reviews-button` - Button - Navigates to My Reviews page.\n  - `waitlist-button` - Button - Navigates to Waitlist page.\n  - `profile-button` - Button - Navigates to User Profile page.\n\n### 2. Dish Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Dish Details\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dish-details-page` - Div - Container for the dish details page.\n  - `dish-name` - H1 - Displays dish name.\n  - `dish-price` - Div - Displays dish price.\n  - `back-to-menu` - Button - Navigates back to Menu page.\n\n### 4. My Reservations Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reservations\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `my-reservations-page` - Div - Container for the reservations page.\n  - `reservations-table` - Table - Displays reservations with date, time, party size, status.\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` - Button - Cancel a specific reservation.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 6. Waitlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Waitlist\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `waitlist-page` - Div - Container for the waitlist page.\n  - `waitlist-party-size` - Dropdown - Select party size.\n  - `join-waitlist-button` - Button - Join the waitlist.\n  - `user-position` - Div - Displays user's current position on waitlist.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 7. My Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reviews\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reviews-page` - Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - `reviews-list` - Div - Lists reviews with dish name, rating, and text.\n  - `write-new-review-button` - Button - Navigate to Write Review page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 8. Write Review Page\n- **Page Title**: Write Review\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `write-review-page` - Div - Container for write review page.\n  - `select-dish` - Dropdown - Select dish to review.\n  - `rating-input` - Dropdown - Select rating 1-5 stars.\n  - `review-text` - Textarea - Input for review text.\n  - `submit-review-button` - Button - Submit review.\n  - `back-to-reviews` - Button - Navigate back to My Reviews page.\n\n### 9. User Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: My Profile\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `profile-page` - Div - Container for profile page.\n  - `profile-username` - Div - Display username (non-editable).\n  - `profile-email` - Input - Update email.\n  - `update-profile-button` - Button - Save profile changes.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n---\n\n## Navigation Flow\n\n- From Dashboard:\n  - `make-reservation-button` -> Make Reservation page\n  - `view-menu-button` -> Menu page\n  - `my-reservations-button` -> My Reservations page\n  - `my-reviews-button` -> My Reviews page\n  - `waitlist-button` -> Waitlist page\n  - `profile-button` -> User Profile page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` refreshes Dashboard\n\n- From Menu page:\n  - `view-dish-button-{dish_id}` -> Dish Details page for selected dish\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Dish Details page:\n  - `back-to-menu` -> Menu page\n\n- From Make Reservation page:\n  - `submit-reservation-button` -> Submit reservation and return to Dashboard\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reservations page:\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` -> Cancel reservation (remains on page or refresh)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Waitlist page:\n  - `join-waitlist-button` -> Join waitlist (user stays on page to see position)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reviews page:\n  - `write-new-review-button` -> Write Review page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Write Review page:\n  - `submit-review-button` -> Submit review and return to My Reviews page\n  - `back-to-reviews` -> My Reviews page\n\n- From User Profile page:\n  - `update-profile-button` -> Save changes (stay or return to Dashboard)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n---\n\n## Data File Schemas\n\nAll data files are stored in the `data/` directory with pipe (`|`) delimited fields. Each line represents one record.\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- Fields: `username|email|phone|full_name`\n- Types:\n  - username: string\n  - email: string\n  - phone: string\n  - full_name: string\n- Example:\n  ```\n  john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner\n  jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie\n  ```\n\n### 2. menu.txt\n- Fields: `dish_id|name|category|price|description|ingredients|dietary|avg_rating`\n- Types:\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - name: string\n  - category: string\n  - price: float\n  - description: string\n  - ingredients: string (comma-separated list)\n  - dietary: string\n  - avg_rating: float\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5\n  2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8\n  3|Chocolate Lava Cake|Desserts|7.99|Warm chocolate cake with molten center|Chocolate,Flour,Eggs,Sugar|Vegetarian|4.9\n  4|Green Tea|Beverages|3.99|Premium Japanese green tea|Green Tea Leaves,Water|Vegan|4.6\n  ```\n\n### 3. reservations.txt\n- Fields: `reservation_id|username|guest_name|phone|email|party_size|date|time|special_requests|status`\n- Types:\n  - reservation_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - guest_name: string\n  - phone: string\n  - email: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - time: time (HH:MM)\n  - special_requests: string\n  - status: string (e.g., Upcoming, Completed)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming\n  2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed\n  3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming\n  ```\n\n### 4. waitlist.txt\n- Fields: `waitlist_id|username|party_size|join_time|status`\n- Types:\n  - waitlist_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - join_time: datetime (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS)\n  - status: string (e.g., Active)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active\n  2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active\n  ```\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Fields: `review_id|username|dish_id|rating|review_text|review_date`\n- Types:\n  - review_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - rating: integer (1-5)\n  - review_text: string\n  - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21\n  2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20\n  3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19\n  ```\n\n---\n\nThis completes the design specification for the RestaurantReservation web application, covering page layouts, element IDs, navigation, and local data file schemas.\n",

My Reservations Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reservations\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `my-reservations-page` - Div - Container for the reservations page.\n  - `reservations-table` - Table - Displays reservations with date, time, party size, status.\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` - Button - Cancel a specific reservation.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 6. Waitlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Waitlist\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `waitlist-page` - Div - Container for the waitlist page.\n  - `waitlist-party-size` - Dropdown - Select party size.\n  - `join-waitlist-button` - Button - Join the waitlist.\n  - `user-position` - Div - Displays user's current position on waitlist.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 7. My Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reviews\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reviews-page` - Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - `reviews-list` - Div - Lists reviews with dish name, rating, and text.\n  - `write-new-review-button` - Button - Navigate to Write Review page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 8. Write Review Page\n- **Page Title**: Write Review\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `write-review-page` - Div - Container for write review page.\n  - `select-dish` - Dropdown - Select dish to review.\n  - `rating-input` - Dropdown - Select rating 1-5 stars.\n  - `review-text` - Textarea - Input for review text.\n  - `submit-review-button` - Button - Submit review.\n  - `back-to-reviews` - Button - Navigate back to My Reviews page.\n\n### 9. User Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: My Profile\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `profile-page` - Div - Container for profile page.\n  - `profile-username` - Div - Display username (non-editable).\n  - `profile-email` - Input - Update email.\n  - `update-profile-button` - Button - Save profile changes.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n---\n\n## Navigation Flow\n\n- From Dashboard:\n  - `make-reservation-button` -> Make Reservation page\n  - `view-menu-button` -> Menu page\n  - `my-reservations-button` -> My Reservations page\n  - `my-reviews-button` -> My Reviews page\n  - `waitlist-button` -> Waitlist page\n  - `profile-button` -> User Profile page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` refreshes Dashboard\n\n- From Menu page:\n  - `view-dish-button-{dish_id}` -> Dish Details page for selected dish\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Dish Details page:\n  - `back-to-menu` -> Menu page\n\n- From Make Reservation page:\n  - `submit-reservation-button` -> Submit reservation and return to Dashboard\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reservations page:\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` -> Cancel reservation (remains on page or refresh)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Waitlist page:\n  - `join-waitlist-button` -> Join waitlist (user stays on page to see position)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reviews page:\n  - `write-new-review-button` -> Write Review page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Write Review page:\n  - `submit-review-button` -> Submit review and return to My Reviews page\n  - `back-to-reviews` -> My Reviews page\n\n- From User Profile page:\n  - `update-profile-button` -> Save changes (stay or return to Dashboard)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n---\n\n## Data File Schemas\n\nAll data files are stored in the `data/` directory with pipe (`|`) delimited fields. Each line represents one record.\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- Fields: `username|email|phone|full_name`\n- Types:\n  - username: string\n  - email: string\n  - phone: string\n  - full_name: string\n- Example:\n  ```\n  john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner\n  jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie\n  ```\n\n### 2. menu.txt\n- Fields: `dish_id|name|category|price|description|ingredients|dietary|avg_rating`\n- Types:\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - name: string\n  - category: string\n  - price: float\n  - description: string\n  - ingredients: string (comma-separated list)\n  - dietary: string\n  - avg_rating: float\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5\n  2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8\n  3|Chocolate Lava Cake|Desserts|7.99|Warm chocolate cake with molten center|Chocolate,Flour,Eggs,Sugar|Vegetarian|4.9\n  4|Green Tea|Beverages|3.99|Premium Japanese green tea|Green Tea Leaves,Water|Vegan|4.6\n  ```\n\n### 3. reservations.txt\n- Fields: `reservation_id|username|guest_name|phone|email|party_size|date|time|special_requests|status`\n- Types:\n  - reservation_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - guest_name: string\n  - phone: string\n  - email: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - time: time (HH:MM)\n  - special_requests: string\n  - status: string (e.g., Upcoming, Completed)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming\n  2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed\n  3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming\n  ```\n\n### 4. waitlist.txt\n- Fields: `waitlist_id|username|party_size|join_time|status`\n- Types:\n  - waitlist_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - join_time: datetime (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS)\n  - status: string (e.g., Active)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active\n  2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active\n  ```\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Fields: `review_id|username|dish_id|rating|review_text|review_date`\n- Types:\n  - review_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - rating: integer (1-5)\n  - review_text: string\n  - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21\n  2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20\n  3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19\n  ```\n\n---\n\nThis completes the design specification for the RestaurantReservation web application, covering page layouts, element IDs, navigation, and local data file schemas.\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for 'RestaurantReservation' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named 'RestaurantReservation' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse restaurant menus, make table reservations, write reviews, check waitlist status, and manage their dining history. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the 'RestaurantReservation' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe 'RestaurantReservation' web application will consist of the following nine pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured dishes, upcoming reservations, and navigation to other functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: welcome-message** - Type: H1 - Welcome message displaying username.\n  - **ID: make-reservation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to reservation page.\n  - **ID: view-menu-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to menu page.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.\n  - **ID: my-reservations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to my reservations page.\n  - **ID: my-reviews-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to my reviews page.\n  - **ID: waitlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to waitlist page.\n  - **ID: profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to user profile page.\n\n### 2. Menu Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu\n- **Overview**: A page displaying the restaurant menu with categories and filtering.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: menu-page** - Type: Div - Container for the menu page.\n  - **ID: menu-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying dish cards with image, name, price, description.\n  - **ID: view-dish-button-{dish_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view dish details (each card has this).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 3. Dish Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Dish Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific dish.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dish-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dish details page.\n  - **ID: dish-name** - Type: H1 - Display dish name.\n  - **ID: dish-price** - Type: Div - Display dish price.\n  - **ID: back-to-menu** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to menu.\n\n### 4. Make Reservation Page\n- **Page Title**: Make Reservation\n- **Overview**: A page for users to make a table reservation.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: reservation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reservation page.\n  - **ID: guest-name** - Type: Input - Field to input guest name.\n  - **ID: party-size** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select party size (1-10).\n  - **ID: reservation-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select reservation date.\n  - **ID: submit-reservation-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit reservation.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 5. My Reservations Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reservations\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all reservations made by the user.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: my-reservations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my reservations page.\n  - **ID: reservations-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying reservations with date, time, party size, status.\n  - **ID: cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel reservation (each upcoming reservation has this).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 6. Waitlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Waitlist\n- **Overview**: A page for users to join the waitlist and check their position.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: waitlist-page** - Type: Div - Container for the waitlist page.\n  - **ID: waitlist-party-size** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select party size.\n  - **ID: join-waitlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to join waitlist.\n  - **ID: user-position** - Type: Div - Display user's current position in waitlist.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 7. My Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reviews\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all reviews written by the user.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of reviews with dish name, rating, review text.\n  - **ID: write-new-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 8. Write Review Page\n- **Page Title**: Write Review\n- **Overview**: A page for users to write a review for a dish.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: write-review-page** - Type: Div - Container for the write review page.\n  - **ID: select-dish** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select dish to review.\n  - **ID: rating-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select rating (1-5 stars).\n  - **ID: review-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to write review text.\n  - **ID: submit-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit review.\n  - **ID: back-to-reviews** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to my reviews.\n\n### 9. User Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: My Profile\n- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.\n  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).\n  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.\n  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe 'RestaurantReservation' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. User Data\n- **File Name**: `users.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  username|email|phone|full_name\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner\n  jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie\n  ```\n\n### 2. Menu Items Data\n- **File Name**: `menu.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  dish_id|name|category|price|description|ingredients|dietary|avg_rating\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5\n  2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8\n  3|Chocolate Lava Cake|Desserts|7.99|Warm chocolate cake with molten center|Chocolate,Flour,Eggs,Sugar|Vegetarian|4.9\n  4|Green Tea|Beverages|3.99|Premium Japanese green tea|Green Tea Leaves,Water|Vegan|4.6\n  ```\n\n### 3. Reservations Data\n- **File Name**: `reservations.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  reservation_id|username|guest_name|phone|email|party_size|date|time|special_requests|status\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming\n  2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed\n  3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming\n  ```\n\n### 4. Waitlist Data\n- **File Name**: `waitlist.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  waitlist_id|username|party_size|join_time|status\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active\n  2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active\n  ```\n\n### 5. Reviews Data\n- **File Name**: `reviews.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  review_id|username|dish_id|rating|review_text|review_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21\n  2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20\n  3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19\n  ```\n\nAll files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing.\n\n\n=== design_spec.md ===\n# RestaurantReservation Web Application Design Specification\n\n---\n\n## Page Layouts and Elements\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Dashboard\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dashboard-page` - Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - `welcome-message` - H1 - Displays welcome message with username.\n  - `make-reservation-button` - Button - Navigates to Make Reservation page.\n  - `view-menu-button` - Button - Navigates to Menu page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Refreshes or navigates to Dashboard page.\n  - `my-reservations-button` - Button - Navigates to My Reservations page.\n  - `my-reviews-button` - Button - Navigates to My Reviews page.\n  - `waitlist-button` - Button - Navigates to Waitlist page.\n  - `profile-button` - Button - Navigates to User Profile page.\n\n### 2. Menu Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `menu-page` - Div - Container for the menu page.\n  - `menu-grid` - Div - Grid displaying dish cards with image, name, price, and description.\n  - `view-dish-button-{dish_id}` - Button - On each dish card; navigates to Dish Details page for that dish.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigates back to Dashboard page.\n\n### 3. Dish Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Dish Details\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dish-details-page` - Div - Container for the dish details page.\n  - `dish-name` - H1 - Displays dish name.\n  - `dish-price` - Div - Displays dish price.\n  - `back-to-menu` - Button - Navigates back to Menu page.\n\n### 4. Make Reservation Page\n- **Page Title**: Make Reservation\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reservation-page` - Div - Container for the reservation page.\n  - `guest-name` - Input - Field for guest name.\n  - `party-size` - Dropdown - Select party size (1-10).\n  - `reservation-date` - Input (date) - Select reservation date.\n  - `submit-reservation-button` - Button - Submit reservation.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 5. My Reservations Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reservations\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `my-reservations-page` - Div - Container for the reservations page.\n  - `reservations-table` - Table - Displays reservations with date, time, party size, status.\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` - Button - Cancel a specific reservation.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 6. Waitlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Waitlist\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `waitlist-page` - Div - Container for the waitlist page.\n  - `waitlist-party-size` - Dropdown - Select party size.\n  - `join-waitlist-button` - Button - Join the waitlist.\n  - `user-position` - Div - Displays user's current position on waitlist.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 7. My Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reviews\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reviews-page` - Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - `reviews-list` - Div - Lists reviews with dish name, rating, and text.\n  - `write-new-review-button` - Button - Navigate to Write Review page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 8. Write Review Page\n- **Page Title**: Write Review\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `write-review-page` - Div - Container for write review page.\n  - `select-dish` - Dropdown - Select dish to review.\n  - `rating-input` - Dropdown - Select rating 1-5 stars.\n  - `review-text` - Textarea - Input for review text.\n  - `submit-review-button` - Button - Submit review.\n  - `back-to-reviews` - Button - Navigate back to My Reviews page.\n\n### 9. User Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: My Profile\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `profile-page` - Div - Container for profile page.\n  - `profile-username` - Div - Display username (non-editable).\n  - `profile-email` - Input - Update email.\n  - `update-profile-button` - Button - Save profile changes.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n---\n\n## Navigation Flow\n\n- From Dashboard:\n  - `make-reservation-button` -> Make Reservation page\n  - `view-menu-button` -> Menu page\n  - `my-reservations-button` -> My Reservations page\n  - `my-reviews-button` -> My Reviews page\n  - `waitlist-button` -> Waitlist page\n  - `profile-button` -> User Profile page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` refreshes Dashboard\n\n- From Menu page:\n  - `view-dish-button-{dish_id}` -> Dish Details page for selected dish\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Dish Details page:\n  - `back-to-menu` -> Menu page\n\n- From Make Reservation page:\n  - `submit-reservation-button` -> Submit reservation and return to Dashboard\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reservations page:\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` -> Cancel reservation (remains on page or refresh)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Waitlist page:\n  - `join-waitlist-button` -> Join waitlist (user stays on page to see position)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reviews page:\n  - `write-new-review-button` -> Write Review page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Write Review page:\n  - `submit-review-button` -> Submit review and return to My Reviews page\n  - `back-to-reviews` -> My Reviews page\n\n- From User Profile page:\n  - `update-profile-button` -> Save changes (stay or return to Dashboard)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n---\n\n## Data File Schemas\n\nAll data files are stored in the `data/` directory with pipe (`|`) delimited fields. Each line represents one record.\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- Fields: `username|email|phone|full_name`\n- Types:\n  - username: string\n  - email: string\n  - phone: string\n  - full_name: string\n- Example:\n  ```\n  john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner\n  jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie\n  ```\n\n### 2. menu.txt\n- Fields: `dish_id|name|category|price|description|ingredients|dietary|avg_rating`\n- Types:\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - name: string\n  - category: string\n  - price: float\n  - description: string\n  - ingredients: string (comma-separated list)\n  - dietary: string\n  - avg_rating: float\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5\n  2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8\n  3|Chocolate Lava Cake|Desserts|7.99|Warm chocolate cake with molten center|Chocolate,Flour,Eggs,Sugar|Vegetarian|4.9\n  4|Green Tea|Beverages|3.99|Premium Japanese green tea|Green Tea Leaves,Water|Vegan|4.6\n  ```\n\n### 3. reservations.txt\n- Fields: `reservation_id|username|guest_name|phone|email|party_size|date|time|special_requests|status`\n- Types:\n  - reservation_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - guest_name: string\n  - phone: string\n  - email: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - time: time (HH:MM)\n  - special_requests: string\n  - status: string (e.g., Upcoming, Completed)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming\n  2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed\n  3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming\n  ```\n\n### 4. waitlist.txt\n- Fields: `waitlist_id|username|party_size|join_time|status`\n- Types:\n  - waitlist_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - join_time: datetime (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS)\n  - status: string (e.g., Active)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active\n  2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active\n  ```\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Fields: `review_id|username|dish_id|rating|review_text|review_date`\n- Types:\n  - review_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - rating: integer (1-5)\n  - review_text: string\n  - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21\n  2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20\n  3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19\n  ```\n\n---\n\nThis completes the design specification for the RestaurantReservation web application, covering page layouts, element IDs, navigation, and local data file schemas.\n",

reservations if r['username'] == CURRENT_USER and r['status'] == 'Upcoming']\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        cancel_id = request.form.get('cancel_id')\n        if cancel_id:\n            cancel_id = int(cancel_id)\n            for r in reservations:\n                if r['reservation_id'] == cancel_id and r['username'] == CURRENT_USER:\n                    r['status'] = 'Cancelled'\n            write_reservations(reservations)\n            return redirect(url_for('my_reservations'))\n    return render_template('my_reservations.html', == 'POST':\n        party_size = int(request.form.get('waitlist-party-size'))\n        if not user_positions:\n            new_id = max([w['waitlist_id'] for w in waitlist_data], default=0) + 1\n            now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')\n            new_waitlist = {\n                'waitlist_id': new_id,\n                'username': CURRENT_USER,\n write_waitlist(waitlist_data)\n            return redirect(url_for('waitlist'))\n\n    return render_template('waitlist.html', user_position=position_index)\n\n@app.route('/my_reviews')\ndef for r in user_reviews:\n        dish = next((d for d in dishes if d['dish_id'] == r['dish_id']), None)\n        r['dish_name'] = dish['name'] if dish else 'Unknown'\n    return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=user_reviews)\n\n@app.route('/write_review', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef write_review():\n    dishes = read_menu()\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n CURRENT_USER,\n            'dish_id': dish_id,\n            'rating': rating,\n            'review_text': review_text,\n            'review_date': today\n        }\n if user:\n            user['email'] = email\n            # Write back all users\n            path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')\n            with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n RestaurantReservation Web Application Design Specification\n\n---\n\n## Page Layouts and Elements\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Dashboard\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dashboard-page` - Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - `welcome-message` - H1 - Displays welcome message with username.\n  - `make-reservation-button` - Button - Navigates to Make Reservation page.\n  - `view-menu-button` - Button - Navigates to Menu page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Refreshes or navigates to Dashboard page.\n  - `my-reservations-button` - Button - Navigates to My Reservations page.\n  - `my-reviews-button` - Button - Navigates to My Reviews page.\n  - `waitlist-button` - Button - Navigates to Waitlist page.\n  - `profile-button` - Button - Navigates to User Profile page.\n\n### 2. Menu Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `menu-page` - Div - Container for the menu page.\n  - `menu-grid` - Div - Grid displaying dish cards with image, name, price, and description.\n  - `view-dish-button-{dish_id}` - Button - On each dish card; navigates to Dish Details page for that dish.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigates back to Dashboard page.\n\n### 3. Dish Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Dish Details\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dish-details-page` - Div - Container for the dish details page.\n  - `dish-name` - H1 - Displays dish name.\n  - `dish-price` - Div - Displays dish price.\n  - `back-to-menu` - Button - Navigates back to Menu page.\n\n### 4. Make Reservation Page\n- **Page Title**: Make Reservation\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reservation-page` - Div - Container for the reservation page.\n  - `guest-name` - Input - Field for guest name.\n  - `party-size` - Dropdown - Select party size (1-10).\n  - `reservation-date` - Input (date) - Select reservation date.\n  - `submit-reservation-button` - Button - Submit reservation.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 5. My Reservations Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reservations\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `my-reservations-page` - Div - Container for the reservations page.\n  - `reservations-table` - Table - Displays reservations with date, time, party size, status.\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` - Button - Cancel a specific reservation.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 6. Waitlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Waitlist\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `waitlist-page` - Div - Container for the waitlist page.\n  - `waitlist-party-size` - Dropdown - Select party size.\n  - `join-waitlist-button` - Button - Join the waitlist.\n  - `user-position` - Div - Displays user's current position on waitlist.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 7. My Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reviews\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reviews-page` - Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - `reviews-list` - Div - Lists reviews with dish name, rating, and text.\n  - `write-new-review-button` - Button - Navigate to Write Review page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 8. Write Review Page\n- **Page Title**: Write Review\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `write-review-page` - Div - Container for write review page.\n  - `select-dish` - Dropdown - Select dish to review.\n  - `rating-input` - Dropdown - Select rating 1-5 stars.\n  - `review-text` - Textarea - Input for review text.\n  - `submit-review-button` - Button - Submit review.\n  - `back-to-reviews` - Button - Navigate back to My Reviews page.\n\n### 9. User Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: My Profile\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `profile-page` - Div - Container for profile page.\n  - `profile-username` - Div - Display username (non-editable).\n  - `profile-email` - Input - Update email.\n  - `update-profile-button` - Button - Save profile changes.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n---\n\n## Navigation Flow\n\n- From Dashboard:\n  - `make-reservation-button` -> Make Reservation page\n  - `view-menu-button` -> Menu page\n  - `my-reservations-button` -> My Reservations page\n  - `my-reviews-button` -> My Reviews page\n  - `waitlist-button` -> Waitlist page\n  - `profile-button` -> User Profile page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` refreshes Dashboard\n\n- From Menu page:\n  - `view-dish-button-{dish_id}` -> Dish Details page for selected dish\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Dish Details page:\n  - `back-to-menu` -> Menu page\n\n- From Make Reservation page:\n  - `submit-reservation-button` -> Submit reservation and return to Dashboard\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reservations page:\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` -> Cancel reservation (remains on page or refresh)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Waitlist page:\n  - `join-waitlist-button` -> Join waitlist (user stays on page to see position)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reviews page:\n  - `write-new-review-button` -> Write Review page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Write Review page:\n  - `submit-review-button` -> Submit review and return to My Reviews page\n  - `back-to-reviews` -> My Reviews page\n\n- From User Profile page:\n  - `update-profile-button` -> Save changes (stay or return to Dashboard)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n---\n\n## Data File Schemas\n\nAll data files are stored in the `data/` directory with pipe (`|`) delimited fields. Each line represents one record.\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- Fields: `username|email|phone|full_name`\n- Types:\n  - username: string\n  - email: string\n  - phone: string\n  - full_name: string\n- Example:\n  ```\n  john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner\n  jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie\n  ```\n\n### 2. menu.txt\n- Fields: `dish_id|name|category|price|description|ingredients|dietary|avg_rating`\n- Types:\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - name: string\n  - category: string\n  - price: float\n  - description: string\n  - ingredients: string (comma-separated list)\n  - dietary: string\n  - avg_rating: float\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5\n  2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8\n  3|Chocolate Lava Cake|Desserts|7.99|Warm chocolate cake with molten center|Chocolate,Flour,Eggs,Sugar|Vegetarian|4.9\n  4|Green Tea|Beverages|3.99|Premium Japanese green tea|Green Tea Leaves,Water|Vegan|4.6\n  ```\n\n### 3. reservations.txt\n- Fields: `reservation_id|username|guest_name|phone|email|party_size|date|time|special_requests|status`\n- Types:\n  - reservation_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - guest_name: string\n  - phone: string\n  - email: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - time: time (HH:MM)\n  - special_requests: string\n  - status: string (e.g., Upcoming, Completed)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming\n  2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed\n  3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming\n  ```\n\n### 4. waitlist.txt\n- Fields: `waitlist_id|username|party_size|join_time|status`\n- Types:\n  - waitlist_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - join_time: datetime (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS)\n  - status: string (e.g., Active)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active\n  2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active\n  ```\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Fields: `review_id|username|dish_id|rating|review_text|review_date`\n- Types:\n  - review_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - rating: integer (1-5)\n  - review_text: string\n  - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21\n  2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20\n  3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19\n  ```\n\n---\n\nThis completes the design specification for the RestaurantReservation web application, covering page layouts, element IDs, navigation, and local data file schemas.\n\n=== app.py ===\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for\nimport os\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\napp = Flask(__name__)\n\nDATA_DIR = 'data'\n\n# Simulate logged in user\nCURRENT_USER = 'john_diner'\n\n# --- Helper functions for file I/O and data parsing ---\n\ndef read_users():\n    users = {}\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')\n    if os.path.exists(path):\n        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if not line:\n                    continue\n                parts = line.split('|')\n                if len(parts) == 4:\n                    username, email, phone, full_name = parts\n                    users[username] = RestaurantReservation Web Application Design Specification\n\n---\n\n## Page Layouts and Elements\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Dashboard\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dashboard-page` - Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - `welcome-message` - H1 - Displays welcome message with username.\n  - `make-reservation-button` - Button - Navigates to Make Reservation page.\n  - `view-menu-button` - Button - Navigates to Menu page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Refreshes or navigates to Dashboard page.\n  - `my-reservations-button` - Button - Navigates to My Reservations page.\n  - `my-reviews-button` - Button - Navigates to My Reviews page.\n  - `waitlist-button` - Button - Navigates to Waitlist page.\n  - `profile-button` - Button - Navigates to User Profile page.\n\n### 2. Menu Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `menu-page` - Div - Container for the menu page.\n  - `menu-grid` - Div - Grid displaying dish cards with image, name, price, and description.\n  - `view-dish-button-{dish_id}` - Button - On each dish card; navigates to Dish Details page for that dish.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigates back to Dashboard page.\n\n### 3. Dish Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Dish Details\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dish-details-page` - Div - Container for the dish details page.\n  - `dish-name` - H1 - Displays dish name.\n  - `dish-price` - Div - Displays dish price.\n  - `back-to-menu` - Button - Navigates back to Menu page.\n\n### 4. Make Reservation Page\n- **Page Title**: Make Reservation\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reservation-page` - Div - Container for the reservation page.\n  - `guest-name` - Input - Field for guest name.\n  - `party-size` - Dropdown - Select party size (1-10).\n  - `reservation-date` - Input (date) - Select reservation date.\n  - `submit-reservation-button` - Button - Submit reservation.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 5. My Reservations Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reservations\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `my-reservations-page` - Div - Container for the reservations page.\n  - `reservations-table` - Table - Displays reservations with date, time, party size, status.\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` - Button - Cancel a specific reservation.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 6. Waitlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Waitlist\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `waitlist-page` - Div - Container for the waitlist page.\n  - `waitlist-party-size` - Dropdown - Select party size.\n  - `join-waitlist-button` - Button - Join the waitlist.\n  - `user-position` - Div - Displays user's current position on waitlist.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 7. My Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: My Reviews\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reviews-page` - Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - `reviews-list` - Div - Lists reviews with dish name, rating, and text.\n  - `write-new-review-button` - Button - Navigate to Write Review page.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n### 8. Write Review Page\n- **Page Title**: Write Review\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `write-review-page` - Div - Container for write review page.\n  - `select-dish` - Dropdown - Select dish to review.\n  - `rating-input` - Dropdown - Select rating 1-5 stars.\n  - `review-text` - Textarea - Input for review text.\n  - `submit-review-button` - Button - Submit review.\n  - `back-to-reviews` - Button - Navigate back to My Reviews page.\n\n### 9. User Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: My Profile\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `profile-page` - Div - Container for profile page.\n  - `profile-username` - Div - Display username (non-editable).\n  - `profile-email` - Input - Update email.\n  - `update-profile-button` - Button - Save profile changes.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` - Button - Navigate back to Dashboard.\n\n---\n\n## Navigation Flow\n\n- From Dashboard:\n  - `make-reservation-button` -> Make Reservation page\n  - `view-menu-button` -> Menu page\n  - `my-reservations-button` -> My Reservations page\n  - `my-reviews-button` -> My Reviews page\n  - `waitlist-button` -> Waitlist page\n  - `profile-button` -> User Profile page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` refreshes Dashboard\n\n- From Menu page:\n  - `view-dish-button-{dish_id}` -> Dish Details page for selected dish\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Dish Details page:\n  - `back-to-menu` -> Menu page\n\n- From Make Reservation page:\n  - `submit-reservation-button` -> Submit reservation and return to Dashboard\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reservations page:\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` -> Cancel reservation (remains on page or refresh)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Waitlist page:\n  - `join-waitlist-button` -> Join waitlist (user stays on page to see position)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From My Reviews page:\n  - `write-new-review-button` -> Write Review page\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n- From Write Review page:\n  - `submit-review-button` -> Submit review and return to My Reviews page\n  - `back-to-reviews` -> My Reviews page\n\n- From User Profile page:\n  - `update-profile-button` -> Save changes (stay or return to Dashboard)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> Dashboard page\n\n---\n\n## Data File Schemas\n\nAll data files are stored in the `data/` directory with pipe (`|`) delimited fields. Each line represents one record.\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- Fields: `username|email|phone|full_name`\n- Types:\n  - username: string\n  - email: string\n  - phone: string\n  - full_name: string\n- Example:\n  ```\n  john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner\n  jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie\n  ```\n\n### 2. menu.txt\n- Fields: `dish_id|name|category|price|description|ingredients|dietary|avg_rating`\n- Types:\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - name: string\n  - category: string\n  - price: float\n  - description: string\n  - ingredients: string (comma-separated list)\n  - dietary: string\n  - avg_rating: float\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5\n  2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8\n  3|Chocolate Lava Cake|Desserts|7.99|Warm chocolate cake with molten center|Chocolate,Flour,Eggs,Sugar|Vegetarian|4.9\n  4|Green Tea|Beverages|3.99|Premium Japanese green tea|Green Tea Leaves,Water|Vegan|4.6\n  ```\n\n### 3. reservations.txt\n- Fields: `reservation_id|username|guest_name|phone|email|party_size|date|time|special_requests|status`\n- Types:\n  - reservation_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - guest_name: string\n  - phone: string\n  - email: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - time: time (HH:MM)\n  - special_requests: string\n  - status: string (e.g., Upcoming, Completed)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming\n  2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed\n  3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming\n  ```\n\n### 4. waitlist.txt\n- Fields: `waitlist_id|username|party_size|join_time|status`\n- Types:\n  - waitlist_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - party_size: integer\n  - join_time: datetime (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS)\n  - status: string (e.g., Active)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active\n  2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active\n  ```\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Fields: `review_id|username|dish_id|rating|review_text|review_date`\n- Types:\n  - review_id: integer\n  - username: string\n  - dish_id: integer\n  - rating: integer (1-5)\n  - review_text: string\n  - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21\n  2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20\n  3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19\n  ```\n\n---\n\nThis completes the design specification for the RestaurantReservation web application, covering page layouts, element IDs, navigation, and local data file schemas.\n\n=== app.py ===\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for\nimport os\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\napp = Flask(__name__)\n\nDATA_DIR = 'data'\n\n# Simulate logged in user\nCURRENT_USER = 'john_diner'\n\n# --- Helper functions for file I/O and data parsing ---\n\ndef read_users():\n    users = {}\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')\n    if os.path.exists(path):\n        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if not line:\n                    continue\n                parts = line.split('|')\n                if len(parts) == 4:\n                    username, email, phone, full_name = parts\n                    users[username] = {\n                        'username': username,\n                        'email': email,\n                        'phone': phone,\n                        'full_name': full_name\n                    }\n    return users\n\ndef read_menu():\n    dishes = []\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'menu.txt')\n    if os.path.exists(path):\n        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if not line:\n                    continue\n                parts = line.split('|')\n                if len(parts) == 8:\n                    dish = {\n                        'dish_id': int(parts[0]),\n                        'name': parts[1],\n                        'category': parts[2],\n                        'price': float(parts[3]),\n                        'description': parts[4],\n                        'ingredients': parts[5],\n                        'dietary': parts[6],\n                        'avg_rating': float(parts[7])\n                    }\n                    dishes.append(dish)\n    return dishes\n\ndef read_reservations():\n    reservations = []\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt')\n    if os.path.exists(path):\n        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line=line.strip()\n                if not line:\n                    continue\n                parts = line.split('|')\n                if len(parts) == 10:\n                    reservation = {\n                        'reservation_id': int(parts[0]),\n                        'username': parts[1],\n                        'guest_name': parts[2],\n                        'phone': parts[3],\n                        'email': parts[4],\n                        'party_size': int(parts[5]),\n                        'date': parts[6],\n                        'time': parts[7],\n                        'special_requests': parts[8],\n                        'status': parts[9]\n                    }\n                    reservations.append(reservation)\n    return reservations\n\ndef write_reservations(reservations):\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt')\n    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n        for r in reservations:\n            line = f\"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['guest_name']}|{r['phone']}|{r['email']}|{r['party_size']}|{r['date']}|{r['time']}|{r['special_requests']}|{r['status']}\\n\"\n            f.write(line)\n\ndef read_waitlist():\n    waitlist = []\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'waitlist.txt')\n    if os.path.exists(path):\n        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line=line.strip()\n                if not line:\n                    continue\n                parts = line.split('|')\n                if len(parts) == 5:\n                    w = {\n                        'waitlist_id': int(parts[0]),\n                        'username': parts[1],\n                        'party_size': int(parts[2]),\n                        'join_time': parts[3],\n                        'status': parts[4]\n                    }\n                    waitlist.append(w)\n    return waitlist\n\ndef write_waitlist(waitlist):\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'waitlist.txt')\n    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n        for w in waitlist:\n            line = f\"{w['waitlist_id']}|{w['username']}|{w['party_size']}|{w['join_time']}|{w['status']}\\n\"\n            f.write(line)\n\ndef read_reviews():\n    reviews = []\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt')\n    if os.path.exists(path):\n        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line=line.strip()\n                if not line:\n                    continue\n                parts = line.split('|')\n                if len(parts) == 6:\n                    review = {\n                        'review_id': int(parts[0]),\n                        'username': parts[1],\n                        'dish_id': int(parts[2]),\n                        'rating': int(parts[3]),\n                        'review_text': parts[4],\n                        'review_date': parts[5]\n                    }\n                    reviews.append(review)\n    return reviews\n\ndef write_reviews(reviews):\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt')\n    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n        for r in reviews:\n            line = f\"{r['review_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['dish_id']}|{r['rating']}|{r['review_text']}|{r['review_date']}\\n\"\n            f.write(line)\n\n# --- Routes ---\n\n@app.route('/')\ndef dashboard():\n    users = read_users()\n    user = users.get(CURRENT_USER, {})\n    return render_template('dashboard.html', username=user.get('full_name', CURRENT_USER))\n\n@app.route('/menu')\ndef menu():\n    dishes = read_menu()\n    return render_template('menu.html', dishes=dishes)\n\n@app.route('/dish/<int:dish_id>')\ndef dish_details(dish_id):\n    dishes = read_menu()\n    dish = next((d for d in dishes if d['dish_id'] == dish_id), None)\n    if dish is None:\n        return \"Dish not found\", 404\n    return render_template('dish_details.html', dish=dish)\n\n@app.route('/make_reservation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef make_reservation():\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        guest_name = request.form.get('guest-name')\n        party_size = int(request.form.get('party-size'))\n        reservation_date = request.form.get('reservation-date')\n        # For simplicity, we assign default phone and email from user\n        users = read_users()\n        user = users.get(CURRENT_USER, {})\n        phone = user.get('phone', '')\n        email = user.get('email', '')\n        reservations = read_reservations()\n        new_id = max([r['reservation_id'] for r in reservations], default=0) + 1\n        new_reservation = {\n            'reservation_id': new_id,\n            'username': CURRENT_USER,\n            'guest_name': guest_name,\n            'phone': phone,\n            'email': email,\n            'party_size': party_size,\n            'date': reservation_date,\n            'time': '19:00',\n            'special_requests': '',\n            'status': 'Upcoming'\n        }\n        reservations.append(new_reservation)\n        write_reservations(reservations)\n        return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))\n    return render_template('make_reservation.html')\n\n@app.route('/my_reservations', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef my_reservations():\n    reservations = read_reservations()\n    user_reservations = [r for r in reservations if r['username'] == CURRENT_USER and r['status'] == 'Upcoming']\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        cancel_id = request.form.get('cancel_id')\n        if cancel_id:\n            cancel_id = int(cancel_id)\n            for r in reservations:\n                if r['reservation_id'] == cancel_id and r['username'] == CURRENT_USER:\n                    r['status'] = 'Cancelled'\n            write_reservations(reservations)\n            return redirect(url_for('my_reservations'))\n    return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservations=user_reservations)\n\n@app.route('/waitlist', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef waitlist():\n    waitlist_data = read_waitlist()\n    user_positions = [w for w in waitlist_data if w['username'] == CURRENT_USER and w['status'] == 'Active']\n    user_position = None\n    if user_positions:\n        user_position = sorted(user_positions, key=lambda w: w['join_time'])[0]\n        position_index = sorted([w for w in waitlist_data if w['status'] == 'Active'], key=lambda w: w['join_time']).index(user_position) + 1\n    else:\n        position_index = None\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        party_size = int(request.form.get('waitlist-party-size'))\n        if not user_positions:\n            new_id = max([w['waitlist_id'] for w in waitlist_data], default=0) + 1\n            now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')\n            new_waitlist = {\n                'waitlist_id': new_id,\n                'username': CURRENT_USER,\n                'party_size': party_size,\n                'join_time': now_str,\n                'status': 'Active'\n            }\n            waitlist_data.append(new_waitlist)\n            write_waitlist(waitlist_data)\n            return redirect(url_for('waitlist'))\n\n    return render_template('waitlist.html', user_position=position_index)\n\n@app.route('/my_reviews')\ndef my_reviews():\n    reviews = read_reviews()\n    dishes = read_menu()\n    # Filter user reviews\n    user_reviews = [r for r in reviews if r['username'] == CURRENT_USER]\n    # Map dish names\n    for r in user_reviews:\n        dish = next((d for d in dishes if d['dish_id'] == r['dish_id']), None)\n        r['dish_name'] = dish['name'] if dish else 'Unknown'\n    return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=user_reviews)\n\n@app.route('/write_review', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef write_review():\n    dishes = read_menu()\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        dish_id = int(request.form.get('select-dish'))\n        rating = int(request.form.get('rating-input'))\n        review_text = request.form.get('review-text')\n        reviews = read_reviews()\n        new_id = max([r['review_id'] for r in reviews], default=0) + 1\n        today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n        new_review = {\n            'review_id': new_id,\n            'username': CURRENT_USER,\n            'dish_id': dish_id,\n            'rating': rating,\n            'review_text': review_text,\n            'review_date': today\n        }\n        reviews.append(new_review)\n        write_reviews(reviews)\n        return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))\n    return render_template('write_review.html', dishes=dishes)\n\n@app.route('/profile', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef profile():\n    users = read_users()\n    user = users.get(CURRENT_USER, {})\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        email = request.form.get('profile-email')\n        if user:\n            user['email'] = email\n            # Write back all users\n            path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')\n            with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                for u in users.values():\n                    line = f\"{u['username']}|{u['email']}|{u['phone']}|{u['full_name']}\\n\"\n                    f.write(line)\n        return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))\n    return render_template('profile.html', user=user)\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    os.makedirs(DATA_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n    app.run(debug=True)\n\n\n===
